21-23 Point Standard Decklists
==============================



 Posted in [PRO TOUR SHADOWS OVER INNISTRAD](/en/events/coverage/ptsoi)
 on April 24, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff












 A total of 33 players earned 21 or 22 points in the Standard rounds of Pro Tour *Shadows over Innistrad*. There were 30 players who earned 21 points (7-3) from Standard and three who earned 22 points (7-2-1). No one earned 23 points.





---


**The following players finished with 22 points (7-2-1) in Standard:**











#### Ondrej Stráský: White-Green Tokens


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
